000659_wps_​conceptual_​model
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_wps_conceptual_model" obligation="normative">
<title>WPS Conceptual Model</title>
<p id="_1c14361f-2646-84cf-34d9-5c61274b4bd4">The WPS service model defines basic properties of any WPS server. A WPS server is a web service that provides access to pre-defined processes and provides job control operations to instantiate, control and monitor processing jobs (<xref target="fig-artifacts-of-the-wps"/>).</p>

<figure id="fig-artifacts-of-the-wps">
2



000977_wps_​native_process_​model
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_wps_native_process_model" obligation="normative">
<title>WPS Native Process Model</title>
<p id="_8ea9e584-3a96-7308-ee35-5179d874f86f">The WPS native process model is a realization of the abstract process model defined in <xref target="subsec-abstract-process-model"/>. The native process model breaks down into the following components:</p>

<ol id="_5283bdf7-5313-deec-372c-528be373ec8a" type="arabic"> <li> <p id="_dbf5bf49-13a0-7fe1-b4e5-3b11500bd984">A general structure for process interface descriptions (<xref target="subsec-common-description-type"/>, <xref target="subsec-process-description"/>) that support process discovery and cataloging</p>
2



001143subsec-data-types
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="subsec-data-types" obligation="normative">
<title>Data Types</title>
<p id="_69c2ac3f-e595-327c-72bd-d2dc2e34be59">This specification defines three common data types for process input and output data (<xref target="fig-io-data-types-overview"/>):</p>

<ol id="_7dc74686-9c46-2595-0e5a-060dc029f5bc" type="arabic"> <li> <p id="_13ad35fa-6f1b-3459-c4c2-1823d622d8d8">ComplexData, such as GML or geo-referenced imagery. This type is kept generic regarding the content and may be extended to provide more detailed domain-specific information.</p>
2



001170_complex_​data
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_complex_data" obligation="normative">
<title>Complex data</title>
<p id="_d7247072-4324-dcb7-a542-954df90a1eef">The ComplexData type does not describe the particular structure for value encoding. Instead, the passed values must comply with the given format and the extended information, if provided.</p>

<requirement id="_9f9bec4e-edbd-d6d2-b5b4-c5ae836ccbd3" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Derived encoding and software implementation</subject>

001221_literal_​data
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_literal_data" obligation="normative">
<title>Literal Data</title>
<p id="_6103c5cd-b503-bcf3-10ca-b5ede8fe79a1">The LiteralData type encodes atomic data such as scalars, linear units, or well-known names. Domains for LiteralData are a combination of data types (e.g. Double, Integer, String), a given value range, and an associated unit (e.g. meters, degrees Celsius).</p>

<requirement id="_084e5ccd-cba9-de1b-8bf4-a3ea4c09b669" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Derived encoding and software implementation</subject>
2



001393_​boundingbox_data
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_boundingbox_data" obligation="normative">
<title>BoundingBox Data</title>
<p id="_1eb43725-9d6b-1581-bbcc-93eec0ea6592">Bounding box data serves a variety of purposes in spatial data processing. Some simple applications are the definition of extents for a clipping operation or the definition of an analysis region. This specification inherits the bounding box specification from OWS Common.</p>

<requirement id="_45798956-62a9-f627-1fa3-e489db24438b" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Derived encoding and software implementation</subject>
2



001593subsec-process-profiles
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="subsec-process-profiles" obligation="normative">
<title>Process Profiles</title>
<p id="_47652adb-647a-253a-f0f5-b5ef30e643ac">Process profiles are blueprints for process implementations and are meant to harmonize process implementations to a certain degree. They serve as a reference for process implementations by providing a description of what the process actually does. While this specification does not attempt to enforce or suggest any particular process profiles, it provides a mechanism to define common processing functionality within the scope of WPS, thus supporting basic process cataloguing and retrieval tasks for distributed processing infrastructures. Depending on the degree of harmonization, the definitions of process profiles may be used to foster a common understanding of widely used processing functions. However, they may also be used to harmonize the technical details of process interfaces and thus document particular interoperability arrangements between process providers and consumers.</p>

<requirement id="_9488f66d-a7fe-d42f-44fe-a72e5367b083" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Derived encoding and software implementation</subject>
2

002010_common_​wps_service_​model
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_common_wps_service_model" obligation="normative">
<title>Common WPS Service Model</title>
<p id="_32578a1f-28a9-339a-250b-776ae652157e">A Web Processing Service consists of processes and service operations. By definition, processes represent the computational functionality of a WPS, while service operations are used to interact with the WPS and in particular to use the service’s process offerings.</p>

<requirement id="_29a322b9-8c36-8122-5559-f80742ac22be" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Software implementation</subject>
2



002400subsec-getcapabilities-operation
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="subsec-getcapabilities-operation" obligation="normative">
<title>GetCapabilities Operation</title>
<p id="_9bbcbdb9-88f3-8e34-9f7a-0e8e76d2bda9">Per OGC 06-121r9, a GetCapabilities operation is required for any OGC Web service. For WPS, this operation allows a client to retrieve service metadata, basic process offerings, and the available processes present on a WPS server.</p>

<requirement id="_3552bf66-39d6-e9bb-f4e2-55a719d1a320" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Software implementation</subject>

002680subsec-execute-operation
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="subsec-execute-operation" obligation="normative">
<title>Execute Operation</title>
<p id="_ab955a9c-1c2b-0f53-7454-897c93f8461a">The Execute operation allows WPS clients to run a specified process implemented by a server, using the input parameter values provided and returning the output values produced. Inputs may be included directly in the Execute request (by value), or reference web accessible resources (by reference). The outputs may be returned in the form of an XML response document, either embedded within the response document or stored as web accessible resources. Alternatively, for a single output, the server may be directed to return that output in its raw form without being wrapped in an XML response document. This is illustrated in <xref target="fig-execute-response-document-raw-uml"/>.</p>

<figure id="fig-execute-response-document-raw-uml">
2

003277_httpget_​kvp_​binding
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_httpget_kvp_binding" obligation="normative">
<title>HTTP/GET + KVP Binding</title>
<p id="_e8ad8feb-5434-b209-7c7f-56004178bcc7">This section specifies the encoding of WPS requests using HTTP/GET and KVP. Since different HTTP client and server libraries may restrict the size of the URL this binding should only be used if the resulting HTTP/GET URL is reasonably short. The HTTP/GET + KVP binding is only defined for the operations GetCapabilities, DescribeProcess, GetStatus, and GetResult.<fn reference="10"> <p id="_87969567-63a3-3bdd-82a3-d15c99f4ef22">There is no HTTP/GET + KVP binding for execute requests due to the complex and nested structure of the request.</p>
</fn>.</p>

2



003484_dismiss_​extension
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_dismiss_extension" obligation="normative">
<title>Dismiss Extension</title>
<p id="_34d3a364-53b8-4842-06d8-ae29170381bd">The dismiss extension for WPS allows a client to communicate to the server that he is no longer interested in the results of a job. In this case, the server may free all associated resources and “forget” the JobID (<xref target="fig-dismiss-operation-uml"/>). For jobs that are still running, the server may cancel the execution at any time. For jobs that were already finished, the associated status information and the stored results may be deleted without further notice, regardless of the expiration time given in the last status report.</p>

<figure id="fig-dismiss-operation-uml">
2



003492_dismiss_​operation

<title>Dismiss Operation</title>
<p id="_9dd7c6f1-865f-9028-fc90-af4ad40b2ca4">The dismiss operation is a job control operation. Its availability is indicated per process using the jobControlOptions in the ProcessSummary and the ProcessOffering structures.</p>

<requirement id="_13808169-a3a2-c58c-89c0-d0c178807a0d" model="ogc" obligation="requirement" type="class"> <subject>Derived encoding and software implementation</subject>
